harness-eval","697:description: This skill should be used when the user asks to \"test the harness\", \"run integration tests\", \"validate features with real API\", \"test with real model calls\", \"run agent loop tests\", \"verify end-to-end\", or needs to verify OpenHarness features on a real codebase with actual LLM calls.","698-version: 0.2.0","699----","700-","701-# Harness Eval — End-to-End Feature Validation","702-","--","703:Validate OpenHarness features by running real agent loops against an unfamiliar codebase with actual LLM API calls. Every test exercises the full stack: API client → model → tool calls → execution → result.","704-","705-## Core Principles","706-","707-1. **Test on an unfamiliar project** — never test on OpenHarness itself (the agent modifies its own code). Clone a real project as the workspace.","708-2. **Use real API calls** — no mocks. Configure a real LLM endpoint.","--","709-3. **Multi-turn conversations** — always test 2+ turns where the model needs prior context.","710-4. **Combine features** — test hooks+skills+agent loop together, not in isolation.","711-5. **Verify tool execution** — inspect tool call lists and output files, not just model text.","712-","--","713-## Workflow","714-","--","715-### 1. Prepare Workspace","--","716-","--","747-Then run a minimal smoke check through OpenHarness, not just raw `srt`, so you verify the real adapter path:","748-","749-```python","750-from pathlib import Path","751-from openharness.config.settings import Settings, SandboxSettings, save_settings","752:from openharness.tools.bash_tool import BashTool","753-","754-cfg = Path(\"/tmp/openharness-sandbox-settings.json\")","755-save_settings(Settings(sandbox=SandboxSettings(enabled=True, fail_if_unavailable=True)), cfg)","756-# Point config loader at this file, then run BashTool on a tiny command such as `pwd`.","757-```","--","758-","759-If sandbox dependencies are missing, treat that as an environment/setup failure, not a feature regression.","760-","761-### 4. Design Tests","762-","763:Each test follows this pattern:","764-","765-```python","766-engine = make_engine(system_prompt=\"...\", cwd=UNFAMILIAR_PROJECT)","767-evs1 = [ev async for ev in engine.submit_message(\"Read X, analyze Y\")]","768-r1 = collect(evs1)  # text, tools, turns, tokens","--","769-evs2 = [ev async for ev in engine.submit_message(\"Based on what you found...\")]","770-r2 = collect(evs2)","771-assert \"grep\" in r1[\"tools\"]  # verify tools ran","772-```","773-","--","774-For detailed code templates and the `make_engine`/`collect` helpers, consult `references/test-patterns.md`.","775-","776-### 5. Prefer Long-Horizon, Real Agent Loops","--","777-","778-For meaningful end-to-end validation, prefer unfamiliar-repo tasks that force multiple turns, context reuse, and mixed tool usage.","779-","--","788-- Keep polling long-running sessions until they finish; do not abandon a run after the first long pause","789-","790-Recommended long-horizon scenarios:","791-","792-- `architecture_multiturn`","793:  - Turn 1: map architecture, shell/subprocess surfaces, and test entrypoints","794-  - Turn 2: identify top risks and propose refactors","795-  - Turn 3: condense into onboarding or remediation actions","796-  - Success: `bash`, `glob`, `grep`, `read_file` all appear; no timeout; no `MaxTurnsExceeded`","797-","798-- `hook_block_and_recover`","--","802-","803-- `sandbox_multiturn`","804-  - Enable real sandbox settings with `fail_if_unavailable=true`","805-  - First prompt must start with exactly one shell command such as `pwd && ls -la`","806-  - Second prompt must explicitly reuse the prior shell findings","807:  - Success: `bash` executes via sandbox, non-shell tools continue the task, and the agent recovers from incidental repo errors","808-","809-When a scenario fails, classify it before changing code:","810-","811-- `MaxTurnsExceeded`: likely eval harness misconfiguration if `max_turns` was manually lowered","812-- `timeout`: task is too broad or per-prompt timeout is too small","--","814-- tool error with task still completed: feature may still be healthy; inspect recovery behavior","815-","816-### 6. Run Tests","817-","818-```bash","819:python tests/test_merged_prs_on_autoagent.py   # PR feature tests","820-python tests/test_real_large_tasks.py           # large multi-step tasks","821-python tests/test_hooks_skills_plugins_real.py  # hooks/skills/plugins","822-python -m pytest tests/ -q -k \"not autoagent\"  # unit tests (no API)","823-```","824-","--","825-For ad hoc long-horizon validation, it is acceptable to run a temporary Python driver script as long as it:","--","826-","--","827-- uses real OpenHarness engine/tool objects","--","828-- targets an unfamiliar repository","829-- prints per-scenario JSON summaries","830:- records tools, errors, turns, and token usage","831-- stays attached until completion","832-","833-### 7. Interpret Results","834-","835-| Result | Meaning | Action |","--","848-  - Example: missing dependency in the unfamiliar target repo is not automatically an OpenHarness regression","849-  - Example: missing `srt`/`bwrap`/`rg` is an eval environment issue","850-","851-## Feature Coverage Checklist","852-","853:- [ ] Engine: multi-turn memory, tool chaining, parallel tools, error recovery, auto-compaction","854-- [ ] Swarm: InProcessBackend lifecycle, concurrent teammates, coordinator+notifications","855-- [ ] Hooks: pre_tool_use blocking → model adapts, post_tool_use firing","856-- [ ] Skills: skill tool invocation → model follows instructions","857-- [ ] Plugins: plugin-provided skill loaded and used in agent loop","858-- [ ] Memory: YAML frontmatter parsing, body content search, context injection","--","865-- Testing on OpenHarness itself — agent modifies its own running code","866-- Using mocks — misses serialization and API compatibility bugs","867-- Single-turn only — misses context accumulation and compaction bugs","868-- Artificially lowering `max_turns` during real evals — can create false failures that do not reflect product defaults","869-- Not checking tool
